It is usually a beer and a handshake !\"</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">I told him to come along with the outgoing chief engineer after 20 minutes, and in between I whipped up this checklist-- where both chief engineers have to initial every check list item.</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">So , after 20 minues I told both--this is what I want.</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Before the outgoing ex-Moghul line &nbsp;Chief engineer could present his case -- I was NOT handed over this way BLAH BLAH&nbsp; -- I am a reader of body language --&nbsp;</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue;\">I told him \" Listen I caught you red handed&nbsp; \" ARYAING \" a dinner set&nbsp;, along with the crew.&nbsp;( He was dragging it down the alleyway actually-- in a disgraceful manner ) &nbsp;. </span>In 1941, Netaji went to Japan and formed the I.N.A. in 1943. 1945 witnessed the I.N.A. waging a war from the North - West of our country. He inspired his army with the battle cry 'Delhi Chalo'. Even though he did not succeed in this battle, he had driven home his message. The Britishers realised that the Indians were serious about gaining independence, and would assume any VIOLENT means towards that end. On August 17, 1945, Bose died in a plane crash while flying from Bangkok to Tokyo\u2014</i>BLAH BLAH BLAH \u201c.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; </span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>( <i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\">The first being 1.2 million Indian Indentured labour flung all around the planet by the British, as a glorified form of slave labor, which<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; So on 29<sup><span style=\"font-size: x-small;\">th</span></sup> Dec 1942, Japanese promptly shed all secrecy and put him into jail.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; </span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-iHEI-7JJWbU/TjgPt-htoiI/AAAAAAAAE-w/QHhH7jC3h_4/s1600/Japan-Rabaul-5-300x201.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-e3VrnmSkuhc/Tjl_CgWlQWI/AAAAAAAAFCs/Dr0-eU3BGNc/s1600/imagesCA0UOZ1M.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Take a calculator , and work out how many hours a day a person has to work to dig out manually with pick axes and crowbars 620 kilometers of hard rock tunnels on an average of 8 feet high, and 10 feet wide.&nbsp; </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-YwdcIOp0LBc/Tjl-tygwJMI/AAAAAAAAFCg/NZRXe0Vzpoo/s1600/imagesCAA95GED.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">They had 2200 prostitutes shipped in from China, Phillipines and Korea.&nbsp; All of them lived in the tunnels. </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Over the last 9 months , to keep at least one air strip operational the Indians were forced to work in the open even with bombs falling around them.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; They held everything a normal city would hold. </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IbassLFm9l0/TjgWSac2QwI/AAAAAAAAFAc/jm6fdkTfXCw/s1600/yu.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Admiral Yamamoto\u2019s bunker with two circular map rooms was well equipped ( this place stinks as many Western tourists piss there to antagonize the Jap tourists ) . </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-njgHz5BbZLM/T6QLHpn-XmI/AAAAAAAAKrM/gdZnNLzCPp8/s1600/imagesCAOVKN8T.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-njgHz5BbZLM/T6QLHpn-XmI/AAAAAAAAKrM/gdZnNLzCPp8/s1600/imagesCAOVKN8T.jpg\" width=\"296\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-djIzsZkwjnY/TjgQlogeW0I/AAAAAAAAE_M/u-DW3cXjsn8/s1600/imagesCA3I4JF5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"283\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-djIzsZkwjnY/TjgQlogeW0I/AAAAAAAAE_M/u-DW3cXjsn8/s1600/imagesCA3I4JF5.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">Barracks could hold 200000 soldiers. There were 5 airstrips which could be entered from any number of tunnel entrances. Some of these tunnels could hold mini submarines and ships. There were several antiaircraft posts and pill boxes. There were aircraft hangars too.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>Inside were mine , bomb , flame thrower and mortar factories.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-V1_F-Rq3HBc/TjgQsIxz0vI/AAAAAAAAE_Q/7um_RL1-CS4/s1600/imagesCA7B0WQF.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-V1_F-Rq3HBc/TjgQsIxz0vI/AAAAAAAAE_Q/7um_RL1-CS4/s320/imagesCA7B0WQF.jpg\" width=\"257\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\">The Indians died of Malaria, malnutrition, torture ( for NOT completing the daily quota ), big testicle Diphteria ( nicknamed Changi Indian balls ) , sunstroke, dysentery, wet Beriberi, sheer exhaustion\u2014when they died they were just buried at tunnel extremes with displaced rubble.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span></span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"mso-bidi-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-theme-font: minor-latin;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;calibri&quot;;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Only 436 skeletons were exhumed and buried at Port Moresby Bomana Commonwealth war cemetery . Bose's constant passionate declarations to his army INA --that he does NOT have children and hence they are his children must be taken with a pinch of salt-- that is after you do the DN test on his wife and grand children. </span></em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--PNDVRGckgY/T74Barin4dI/AAAAAAAALU4/Tk_3pEgXg2c/s1600/imagesCABEUZJE.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"420\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/--PNDVRGckgY/T74Barin4dI/AAAAAAAALU4/Tk_3pEgXg2c/s400/imagesCABEUZJE.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">Of course your blind servility to Bose may cause you to say that DNA tests are all bull. When the pyre\nwas lit, one of them RK Panda broke down and said, \"\u2026there should have been 13 lakh\npeople here!\"<o:p></o:p></span></span></i><br />\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; How could a penniless hermit\ncould talk so knowledgeably about a city in a foreign country. <o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">\n\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Baba\ninstructed to contact Swami N.G. of INA (Intelligence chief in Germany and SE\nAsia) and see that his daughter Anita should be absolved from stigma.<o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">\n\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">There\nare more than 143 points of similarities between Netaji and Babaji.<o:p></o:p></span></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">\n\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">When\nhe dies his body was draped in <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>tricolour\non the passage to Guptar Ghat.</span> <o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Is 2674 items in 23\nboxes normal for a Sadhu? What about&nbsp;\nGerman Hensoldt binoculars ? British Smith Corona portable typewriter\n?&nbsp; Noritake Japanese tea set ? Same Bruyere pipe\n? Azad Hind Fauj uniform ? &nbsp;Books in Bengali ? Photos of parents and entire family ? Idol of Kali ? Newspaper cuttings of Bose ? &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Books included The\nHistory of the Freedom Movement in India, The Last Days of the Raj, Moscow\u2019s\nShadow Over West Bengal and Solzhenitsyn\u2019s The Gulag Archipelago. This could\nnot be the bedtime reading of a sadhu, right?.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nBose was NOT unfamiliar with such deception.&nbsp;</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nHe had hoodwinked the British and escaped from India to Germany via Afghanistan --</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n-in disguise as a Pathan-- of the deaf and dumb variety.\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-aXmTQr5XfYw/UBZK4_WtJXI/AAAAAAAAOeI/-3kS9rUYgUU/s1600/lofdwq.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"273\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-aXmTQr5XfYw/UBZK4_WtJXI/AAAAAAAAOeI/-3kS9rUYgUU/s1600/lofdwq.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">In the guise of a\nPathan insurance agent (\"Ziaudddin\") to Afghanistan, Bose had travelled\nto Moscow with the passport of an Italian nobleman \"Count Orlando\nMazzotta\". From Moscow he reached Rome and from there he traveled to\nGermany where he instituted the Special Bureau for India under Adam von Trott zu\nSolz, broadcasting on the German-sponsored Azad Hind Radio. He founded the Free\nIndia Centre in Berlin and created the Indian Legion (consisting of some 4500\nsoldiers) out of Indian prisoners of war who had previously fought for the\nBritish in North Africa, but had been captured by Axis forces. The Azad Hind\nlegion was attached to the Waffen SS, and they swore their allegiance to Hitler\nand Bose to secure India's independence.\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fYVjM0WJGIw/UBZLAV0-EgI/AAAAAAAAOeQ/_A8GtJLNUm8/s1600/dfgh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"260\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-fYVjM0WJGIw/UBZLAV0-EgI/AAAAAAAAOeQ/_A8GtJLNUm8/s1600/dfgh.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">In 1941, when Winston\nChurchill learnt that Bose had sought the support of the Axis Powers, he\nfrothed from his mouth in rage, and ordered British agents to assassinate Bose. This remarkable claim comes from\nIrish historian Dr. Eunan O'Halpin, who is the author of several books on\nBritish intelligence and teaches at Trinity College, Dublin.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">British agents were\ninstructed to intercept and eliminate Bose before he reached Germany via the Middle\nEast, according to Professor O'Halpin. According to him, a recently\ndeclassified intelligence document refers to a top-secret instruction to the\nSpecial Operations Executive (SOE) of British intelligence to murder Bose.</span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--hs2iHznAfY/UBZMeXpH0FI/AAAAAAAAOeg/pMDTkWFq5p4/s1600/bjkl;.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--hs2iHznAfY/UBZMeXpH0FI/AAAAAAAAOeg/pMDTkWFq5p4/s640/bjkl;.jpg\" width=\"453\" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">Two SOE operatives in Turkey were instructed\nby their headquarters in London to intercept Bose and kill him before he\nreached Germany. They failed because Bose reached Germany through Central Asia\nand the Soviet Union. Every time the operatives checked back, headquarters told\nthem Churchill's orders were intact and Bose must be found and killed.</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A stenographer, Sham\nLal Jain, deposed before the Khosla Commission that \u2018Pandit Nehru asked him to\nmake typed copies of a hand-written note that said Bose had reached Russia via\nDairen [Manchuria]\u2019. Indians, whowere wounded during air raids,\nhad sand thrown over their bodies.&nbsp;</i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>The treatment by the Japanese was most iniquitous.Under\ncross-examination he said he had <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">joined the Indian National&nbsp;</span></i></span><i style=\"background-color: yellow; font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Army under duress.</i></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">QUOTE--<i> However, according to\nhistorian Yuki Tanaka: \"cannibalism was often a systematic activity\nconducted by whole squads and under the command of officers\". This\nfrequently involved murder for the purpose of securing bodies.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>For example, an Indian\nPOW, Havildar Changdi Ram, testified that: \"[on November 12, 1944] the\nKempeitai beheaded [an Allied] pilot. I saw this from behind a tree and <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">watched\nsome of the Japanese cut flesh from his arms, legs, hips, buttocks and carry it\noff to their quarters... They cut it [into] small pieces and fried it.\"</span><o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>In some cases, flesh\nwas cut from living people: another Indian POW, Lance Naik Hatam Ali (later a\ncitizen of Pakistan), testified that in New Guinea:<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>the Japanese started\nselecting prisoners and <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">every day one prisoner was taken out and killed and\neaten by the soldiers. I personally saw this happen and about 100 prisoners\nwere eaten at this place by the Japanese. T</span>he remainder of us were taken to\nanother spot 50 miles [80 km] away where 10 prisoners died of sickness. At this\nplace, the Japanese again started selecting prisoners to eat. Those selected\nwere taken to a hut where their flesh was cut from their bodies while they were\nalive and they were thrown into a ditch where they later died.<o:p></o:p></i></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><br /></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Perhaps the <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">most senior\nofficer convicted of cannibalism was Lt Gen. Yoshio Tachibana</span> (</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;ms gothic&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u7acb\u82b1\u82b3\u592b</span></i><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>,Tachibana Yoshio), who with 11 other\nJapanese personnel was tried in August 1946 in relation to the execution of\nU.S. Navy airmen, and the cannibalism of at least one of them, during August\n1944, on Chichi Jima, in the Bonin Islands. The airmen were beheaded on\nTachibana's orders. As military and international law did not specifically deal\nwith cannibalism, they were tried for murder and \"prevention of honorable\nburial\". <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Tachibana was sentenced to death, and hanged</span>.\"</i>: &nbsp;UNQUOTE<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\nRecently a British General has declared that Japs did cannibalism at Rabaul.(www.antonybeevor.com)<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\">Now, some doodh ka doodh paani ka paani--</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\">The cry <span style=\"color: blue;\">JAI HIND </span>was NOT coined by Netaji Bose. &nbsp;It was made by&nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">Dr Champakaraman Pillai\n, </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\">who formed the Berlin Committee in\nGermany to assist freedom fighters before the 1</span><sup style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; line-height: 150%;\">st</sup><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"> World war . He &nbsp;had\ndirect dealings with Hitler. He died on May 28th, 1934 under suspicious circumstances , because he asked for a written apology from Hitler with a deadline, for derogatory reference to Indians in his book Mein Kamph.. His ashes were scattered\nin Karamana River in Thiruvananthapuram. &nbsp;His ashes could not be brought in before,\ndue to objections from Gandhiji and Nehru . Kodungallur was the centre of festivals during the reign of Hindu king Cheraman Perumal.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>&nbsp;  </b></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>Vedic knowledge was translated into Arabic from Malayalam and Sanskrit at Mecca even before Mohammed was born&nbsp;. <span style=\"color: red;\">This was in great demand at Timbuctoo of Mali, where the wise king Mansa Musa traded large quantities of gold with books</span>.&nbsp;</b></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b><br /></b></span></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><b>All these priceless books in Maths Medicine and Science are kept underground, buried under the dry sands\u2014 to prevent the white man from stealing it, as per the records of Ibn Batuta</b></span>.. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><br /></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-f0nQ4ERdRD4/TjaWsNUY5gI/AAAAAAAAE7M/ZFGmx9sQt80/s1600/imagesCASY8WZ3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; The Russian merchant arrived in India in 1469 and lived in the country for three years, travelling all the way to Kerala and Sri Lanka.<br />\n<br />\nFrom Dabhol, Nikitin traveled to Calicut in what was a 25-day journey --- \u201cCalicut is a big harbor on the Indian Sea, and God forbid that any ship should pass by it; no one who sails past it will cross the sea unscathed,\u201d he wrote. \u201cAnd it produces pepper, ginger, nutmeg, cinnamon, clove, spices, adrak, and many kinds of herbs. Everything is cheap there.\u201d --- \"<br />\n<br />\nhttps://tinyurl.com/y7nvrfem<br />\n============================<br />\n<br />\n-&gt; \"Russia and India: A civilisational friendship. Athanasius (also known as Afanasy) Nikitin was in India nearly thirty years before Vasco da Gama and, in fact, opened the country for Europeans. After Nikitin, however, it took two centuries to establish direct contact between India and Russia. It was only in the late 17th century that Russian merchant Semyon Malenkiy brought a letter from Peter-the-Great to the Badshah, Mughal-Emperor-Aurangzeb, with a request to allow him to sell Russian goods, as well as purchase local products. Her thumb was a blur , typing amazingly fast, with NIL mistakes and deletions.<br />\n<br />\nThis set me thinking.<br />\n<br />\n&nbsp;Her mobile phone keyboard was not <span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">QWERTY.</span>&nbsp;&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">This is a stupid configuration, this planet is stuck with. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2AFktZrdA_M/TnchWMu2gqI/AAAAAAAAGSE/JuZMVNYbztI/s1600/ndw.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2AFktZrdA_M/TnchWMu2gqI/AAAAAAAAGSE/JuZMVNYbztI/s1600/ndw.gif\" /></a></div><br />\nOn modern mobile phone keyboards where you type with one hand, this layout is bullshit.<br />\n<br />\nThis type key layout was&nbsp;designed, when Remington wanted to sell their mechanical typewriters, 140 years ago . So they trained their salesmen to type typewriter , very fast, and WOW all the dumb bumpkin folks. &nbsp;It was easy as fingers needed to type only on the top row. <br />\n<br />\nThe peabrained designer said to himself that as long as he puts QW and ZX at extreme corners on LH side ( as most people were right handed ) he would be called innovative. <br />\n<br />\nIf you notice the keyboard itself is not ergometric. It was meant for human beings with VERY narrow shoulders, who could keep their elbows pressedto their body sides. &nbsp;This means the typist cannot have pectoral muscles. <br />\n<br />\nWhen you have a mechanical typewriter you cannot type too fast , or the keys get entangled.&nbsp; This layout was meant to slow you down deliberately.<br />\n<br />\nThis stupid QWERTY keyboard required most of the typing to be done on the top row, which required the fingers to travel. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8bKDsxhHaXw/TmAUM9uHYHI/AAAAAAAAF4s/9FWOcSF1WIw/s1600/imagesCA6ZURW9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8bKDsxhHaXw/TmAUM9uHYHI/AAAAAAAAF4s/9FWOcSF1WIw/s1600/imagesCA6ZURW9.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\nThe middle row which is the home row should do most of the typing on a efficient system. and the bottom row should do the least-- as it is difficult to reach. Typing should be alternated between two hands.<br />\n<br />\nIt is high time a SPLIT innovative keyboard is made , for real HE men with pectorals. <br />\n<br />\nA typewriter is NO longer a cute typists monopoly--or for the matter a pigeon chested Amol Palekar type babu's.&nbsp; There I met my younger son\u2019s classmate\u2019s father. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">During the course of our polite conversation he asked me I f I knew that my son is getting bullied in school. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I said \u201c <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He is the tallest and heaviest guy in his class- how can anybody <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>dare to bully him.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He replied \u201c Your wife will know the bully, he is the class leader and 4 years older than the rest of the class \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">On the drive back home I asked my wife , whether she knew anything about it. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">She said he has never come home with torn clothes. I asked her about missing pens , not wanting to go to school , or some signs like that.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">She said <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u201c Yes, he does NOT like to go to school. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Sometimes he comes back with his compass box or pen missing . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I have already bought three new ones in the last 3 months. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Certain days he comes back home without eating his lunch packed in the tiffin box. He appears disturbed while studying at home . But the class leader is the boy who gives me notes , whenever Aashik has missed school. Poor chap, his parents are in Dubai and he is all alone , staying with some far off relatives \u201c. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GWwaI-hb_Bg/TjMLAZNWcCI/AAAAAAAAEws/nT7RRe74ER8/s1600/imagesCAG4F0HP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GWwaI-hb_Bg/TjMLAZNWcCI/AAAAAAAAEws/nT7RRe74ER8/s1600/imagesCAG4F0HP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">At home , I confronted my son . He came out with the truth, after some arm twisting . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">My son was the butt of all the <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>practical jokes of the bully -- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>he would throw things at him in class. \u2013 he would be teasing him in front of the whole class and girls constantly\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I told my wife \u201c Tomorrow , though it is a holiday for younger kids --first thing in the morning we will be going to the school and I will speak to the Principal and class teacher \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">At school I told the Principal <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>\u201c I want to speak to you in front of my son\u2019s teachers. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It is about my son getting bullied in your school. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>If I don\u2019t see a good receptive attitude from you, I will put unbearable heat on the school \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pretty soon we had 3 teachers in the Principals room. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I asked them if they knew my son was getting bullied. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">All the 3 of them said <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u201c Yes!. We though you knew. Your son get bullied by children half his size , just because he does NOT retaliate, so they get encouraged \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-G1BCaV65jv4/TjMLFrz6D5I/AAAAAAAAEww/2cq6jvaQgSM/s1600/imagesCAIYWQ7C.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-G1BCaV65jv4/TjMLFrz6D5I/AAAAAAAAEww/2cq6jvaQgSM/s1600/imagesCAIYWQ7C.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I told them \u201c I have hung a sand bag in my house since he was 5 years old. I have taught him personally how to destroy anybody in physical contact OR even to kill a fully grown up adult. But I have told him never ever to attack anybody, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>So may be this is why he is getting bullied. This bullying will stop tomorrow within one hour of school opening\u2014I will do it my way. All I am asking you<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>is to turn a Nelsons eye. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Though my 12 year old son is 5 feet 9 inches tall and 85 <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>kilos in weight , the bully will NOT be hurt, he will only be humiliated \u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I made a hefty donation to the principal\u2019s school fund and we left.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6HQQD7ddZHI/TjMLLkrQd0I/AAAAAAAAEw0/54oh0IZosZY/s1600/imagesCAWWMNKL.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6HQQD7ddZHI/TjMLLkrQd0I/AAAAAAAAEw0/54oh0IZosZY/s1600/imagesCAWWMNKL.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">On the way back my wife asked me \u201c Are you going to tell Aashik to beat up the bully. He can do it very easily, but then what if the bully relatiates by poking his eye with a compass needle ? \u201c <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\"><em>I said \u201c I would rather have a one eyed son , than a coward with my blood running in his veins . This bully works safe in the assumption that there will be NO relatiation . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>At his age of 16, he wants to impress all the 13 year old girls , by taking on a bigger child. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>He suffers from resentment as his parents have left him alone and are in Dubai\" .&nbsp;</em></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">\"<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Bullying gives him release from his frustrations.&nbsp; This is a easy way out to displace internal aggression . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>It makes him feel empowered. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Teasing, playing practical jokes, throwing things at you, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>hiding personal belongings,&nbsp; is all part of the bully\u2019s tactics . <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>The only way out is to take him head on , just once , without hurting him physically \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></em></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YHQ7EZuR8nU/TjMLYcMpBJI/AAAAAAAAEw4/MlCorhR01Rg/s1600/TTT.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YHQ7EZuR8nU/TjMLYcMpBJI/AAAAAAAAEw4/MlCorhR01Rg/s1600/TTT.png\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So after I reached home I told my son <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u201c Tomorrow as soon as you go to school, the bully will start off as usual. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>He is just trying to be a hero in front of the girls by taking on a guy double his size. I want you to do this <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u2013 now watch carefully. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>If you don\u2019t do&nbsp;exactly what<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I tell you, when you come home in the evening I will kick your fuckin' ass. \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">My son cried bitterly , for I was his ultimate hero, and had never beaten him or spoke to him rudely till then. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Next day\u2014he went to school . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The bully came to him with his usual teasing games with the whole class watching.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">My son bent him double, picked him off the ground whirled him around to upset his inner ear cochlea balance, and threw him 8 feet away. He lay there for a couple of minutes <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>totally dazed , picked himself up and came charging . This time my son palmed his jaw, jerked his head backwards to upset the inner ear spirit level again, and shoved him so hard that he went flying again . It took some time for him regain his balance get up and slink away . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">That was it. <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The girls , two dozen of them were the first to start clapping , and then the rest of the class followed . <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This was what all of them wanted. Before he left school for the day , this 16 year old bully taunted my son <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u201c Next time you mother asks me for notes , <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I wont give it to her!\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The word spread <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>all over school like wild fire \u2013 Aashik has beaten up the school bully. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>This came to my wife from several sources. Few parents thanked my wife as the previous year 3 childern left the school, unable to face this type of harassment. Complaining to the teachers made NO difference as the bully's parents were wealthy people from Dubai, and close to a school board member.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-q3z5geWfDEw/TjMLfKPTiYI/AAAAAAAAEw8/pnD35BUI-dE/s1600/imagesCAWXH7KR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-q3z5geWfDEw/TjMLfKPTiYI/AAAAAAAAEw8/pnD35BUI-dE/s1600/imagesCAWXH7KR.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Six days later, a Karate black belt was to come and demonstrate his prowess in breaking tiles, to get more enrollment into the Karate club of school .<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I told my son \u201c After this man finishes, I want you to go on stage and ask for one more tile and break it front of the whole school <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I don\u2019t care if you break your bone \u2014 <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>make sure you do it \u201c <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Immediately my wife held on to my arm, and said \u201c You are NOT gonna confront them . They are just having a ball, in a group. I am telling you. Meri kasam! \u201d<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">She held on to my arm so strong that that spot took 2 weeks to recover from compressed nerves and damaged muscle fibres.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">At half time interval, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>as soon as I saw this gang going out for a smoke, I made an excuse that I have to go and take a leak. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>And then I doubled back to the spot where these trouble makers were sitting in a group , smoking and generally having a ball. They had their tails up, as all were giving them a wide berth.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So I went to them and said \u201c After the interval , when the movie starts, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>I don\u2019t want to hear you guys at all -- <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>If I hear you breathe , just see what I do to you. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>By the way, I am NOT police \u2014 I sit in the front row with my wife and two sons <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u201c <o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When I came back to my seat my wife and two sons asked me \u201c We know you talked to those men .What did you tell them?\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I told the truth \u201c I told them that I don\u2019t want to hear them breathe. I did NOT tell them what I will do to them if they disobey\u2014 that is their problem to figure it out <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Bullies always work on the preconceived notion that there will NOT be a severe price to pay.<span style=\"color: blue;\"> It is this feeling of safety which propels them \u201c<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">20 minutes after the movie started again, the group of 5 quietly melted away in the darkness.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Later my elder genius son , who was never a fan of my tough acting , \u201ctaking on the world alone \u201d <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>tactics , told his mother in private <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>at the airport<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>\u201d There was only one man in that <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>movie hall holding hundreds , who could have silenced that rowdy gang, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>and he did it! \u201d<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">  </span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">Now let me talk about \"<span style=\"color: red;\">bullying at the workplace \"</span>--</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">Before going to Cornell for his ME in computer science, he worked for the biggest computer software company in India for 6 months-- just to get work experience, till he left India.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">He stayed with a brilliant Bihari boy , together in a rented flat. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">So one day my son called me up and asked me if I have some tips for painful stomach ulcers. He said his flatmate, suffers from it. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">So i wanted to know what type of food he eats. My son said he has rarely eaten with him , that he goes to office by 7 AM and comes back at midnight, no Saturdays and Sundays .</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">I had a piece of advise--&nbsp; </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">I told my son never to get&nbsp;USED.&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">He replied that he goes to office at 9AM and comes back by 6 PM-- but the Bihari friend , was being used by his female boss. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">She would constantly shout at him , she would work only between 9 to 5 will NOT come on Saturdays / Sundays . And that all the projects were powered by the fertile brains of his friend -- but she took all the credit personally , as trainees don't count.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">I said \" Tell your friend , that I told him this.&nbsp; Never ever get used.&nbsp; And this type of thing is NOT gonna help his ulcers. He MUST confront this Cruella De Ville.\"</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-KiNln-36_OA/TjOhVbm8CbI/AAAAAAAAExk/l2l7Dd1Hmdw/s1600/imagesCAU3GL91.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-KiNln-36_OA/TjOhVbm8CbI/AAAAAAAAExk/l2l7Dd1Hmdw/s1600/imagesCAU3GL91.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">Next day my excited son calls me up on the ship . </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">He said \" His friend confronted her .&nbsp; He told her that he would report to her boss, that she does NOT have any brains , has&nbsp;NO dang clue what is happening , that she cannot understand the big picture or small picture of current ongoing high profile project with a major US software company, that she is just a parasite / middleman in the work place, but yet&nbsp;hogging all the team effort credit ,&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">-- that she has climbed this far up the ladder this slimy way--&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">but no more !\".</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-9W5FZHIY-BI/TjOhZpjQOjI/AAAAAAAAExo/T6iFAcSxx0w/s1600/imagesCA4CC7UP.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-9W5FZHIY-BI/TjOhZpjQOjI/AAAAAAAAExo/T6iFAcSxx0w/s1600/imagesCA4CC7UP.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">Wonder of wonders--&nbsp; that very hour she applied for 6 months of official long leave and left the office. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">I guess she knew what she was worth. The only way this pretender female&nbsp;boss could continue was by twisting the arm of her team, by harassing, shouting, threatening --</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\"><em>It is your fault if you allow such a thing to happen to you in your workplace. </em></span><br />\n<br />\n<em><span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot;;\">You are entitled to say NO to such mindless abuse.</span>&nbsp;</span></em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; Higher the frequency, higher the perceived pitch. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uBOfdLa37lk/TjEj2G__wMI/AAAAAAAAErU/clPTKowZC1E/s1600/imagesCA23XAO6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-uBOfdLa37lk/TjEj2G__wMI/AAAAAAAAErU/clPTKowZC1E/s1600/imagesCA23XAO6.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nThe wonder of the cilia hairs is that it can perceive 1500 levels of pitch. <br />\n<br />\nThe number of discriminable tones in in the hundreds of thousands.&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nAre you not able to recognise the voice of a long lost friend?&nbsp;&nbsp; Amazing , right? <br />\n<br />\nThe audo frequency range encompasses 9 octaves.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eeGibGulQp4/TjEjg50etnI/AAAAAAAAErI/fa_Kg7KetAQ/s1600/imagesCADUEH6E.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eeGibGulQp4/TjEjg50etnI/AAAAAAAAErI/fa_Kg7KetAQ/s1600/imagesCADUEH6E.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nIf 300 Hz is played in one ear and 310 in the other ear via stereo headphones the binaural frequency will be 10 Hz. He spoke Sanskrit NOT Sinhalese or Malayam, and was supposed to have the equivalent of 10 heads worth Vedic knowledge. <br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: x-large;\">RAVANA IS FROM THE <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">YADU CLAN</span> WHO MIGRATED FROM RIVER SARASWATI&nbsp; BANKS (&nbsp; AT THE SEA DELTA ) DOWN TO KERALA IN 6000 BC.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-GjW6zCGy9cI/TjBikGPAMrI/AAAAAAAAEqw/Y5w28NbSolM/s1600/imagesCACW4NA1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; I remember, when I was 6 years old, our favourite past time used to be, to create light acetylene gas by putting water on Calcium Carbide&nbsp;and fill up 4 huge rubber balloons with this gas, with a silk&nbsp;saree piece in between and then use it as a kite or to jump off a high tree branch.&nbsp; It was a dangerous game, but we are still alive.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-bzYdbguz7Cw/TjBgS_TE5ZI/AAAAAAAAEqE/u4mhsspXdiM/s1600/imagesCAIDJ636.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em;
